; TerminalVector.txt - 8x12 (and 8x13) font bitmaps.
;
; Jason Hood, 6 to 17 October, 2014.
;
; 24 July to 28 August, 2015:
; + completed WGL4 & matched Lucida Console;
; + added a bunch of characters to view translations (diffutils/grep/texinfo);
; + completed Arrows (and tweaked the double diagonal arrows);
; + completed Geometric Shapes;
; + added more Greek letters (some from fixed, changing mine to match);
; + added some more Miscellaneous Symbols;
; + added more IPA characters;
; + added Braille;
; + added four more fractions and the Roman numerals;
; + added a few more Cyrillic letters;
; + added Armenian, Hebrew, Thai, Georgian, Control Pictures, Runes & Katakana
;   Half Width from fixed;
; + added more mathematical/technical symbols;
; + added a couple more combining accents;
; * renamed everything to match AGLFN;
; + added characters missing from AGLFN;
; + completed Super and Sub Scripts, with accompanying modifier letters.
;
; Bitmaps were originally extracted from the 8x12 vga*.fon (and ega80woa.fon)
; files from Windows 7 SP1 (although I don't believe they've changed for quite
; some time).  "Fixed" is Markus Kuhn's UCS updates to X11's misc-fixed 8x13.
; Some bitmaps came from, or were inspired by, Dmitry Bolkhovityanov's Unicode
; VGA font.
;
; The format is simple: each character starts with its Unicode code-point and
; Adobe Glyph List For New Fonts name (if it has one); if there's an 8x13
; bitmap, the first line of that follows the name; anything following is
; ignored, which is the code page the bitmap comes from (if unmodified; 437 is
; vgaoem & 437e is ega80woa) and its Unicode character name.  The next 12 lines
; are the bitmap data: '.' for no pixel, '#' for a pixel, for eight pixels (and
; again if there's an 8x13 bitmap); anything following is ignored.  Unless
; there's an explicit 8x13 bitmap, characters in the range U+2321..U+259F will
; have their top line duplicated.


; The control characters (including U+007F/DELETE) need glyphs so
; WriteConsoleOutputA works the same as a raster font.	However, defining the
; controls seems to interfere with the undefined character, so explicitly use
; U+0001 for that (which WriteConsole still maps to U+263A).

U+0000					NULL
........
........
........
........
........
........
........
........
........
........
